<Text>We have used Lewis Carpet Cleaners a number of times in the past and have been very satisfied.  This last time was a bit different.  We have new carpet that is almost 2 years old. We were scheduled for late afternoon one Friday and the cleaner techs called and said they could come earlier, which was great for me. It was around noon and I suspect, given their surprise at the size of the area, that they weren't so pleased and that maybe they would miss their lunch (just surmising here).  We offered them sodas and water, which they refused.  They were nice enough, but there were a couple red flags.  1) I had called Lewis prior to the cleaning and told him we had 4 FLOR rugs (in addition to some wall-to-wall) to be cleaned and asked if they knew how to do that since they're a bit different from other area rugs.  He told me that FLOR had just indeed called him recently to see if they could refer people to Lewis for FLOR rug cleaning.  I told him I was pleased to know that there would be knowledgeable people cleaning our rugs.  Well, when the tech guys got here, they had no idea what FLOR rugs were.  To their credit, they dug up some plastic tarps from their truck to put under the rugs in case anything leaked through to the engineered wood floor beneath.  They were very careful and all worked out well.  I had to print out the cleaning instructions from FLOR for the guys, but they didn't seem too interested.  Just glad it turned out okay.

2) When I approved the estimate, no other services were explained to me nor was I asked if there was anything else I wanted.  I assumed they would Scotch Guard at the end.  When they were nearly finished, we asked if they would Scotch Guard the carpets, they said they didn't have any in the truck.  ???!!!  The one man, who appeared to be the one in charge, said he was just filling in for someone and had to load the truck quickly that morning and must have forgotten to bring it. No offer was made to go get some.  It can only be done on damp carpets, so there was no way we could wait until the next week and have them come back and do it.

3)We felt that both guys were trying to finish their job asap, especially since they got to us earlier than expected, and were anxious to get off work early on a Friday, although they had one more house to go to after us. We're still not sure about the stairs--but maybe it IS just shadows.They then asked if the cleaners had given us some of their spot cleaner and when we said no, they promptly gave us a bottle.

In sum, it all seemed a bit rushed, and sub-par for Lewis.  No ScothGuard?  Really?  No knowledge of FLOR even though I had stressed that?

< review>
The checkout counter is inside, but there's a gigantic garage-type door open, they are enforcing social distancing, and all the employees are wearing masks, so it feels pretty safe. Their selection and prices are amazing, and they sell things in bags, or by cubic yard. If you're going to get cubic yards of anything, bring a truck, or some very sturdy trash bags and tools to bag it yourself. They have gorilla hair mulch, every other kind of mulch imaginable, river rocks, gravel, topsoil, plus they do custom blends and can deliver. If you are doing any kind of real Landscaping, it's worth the trip.< /review>

This is not a complain about the food or the servive.  This is a complain about the way I can order food here. I wanted to order ten cold sandwiches for pickup.  No, can't do. <Gmap_id>0x80ecc55ccfe20189:0xa1855018c54ee684< /Gmap_id><Pics>None<//Pics><response>None< /response>< Review>
First place I have ever been that charged for Pico De Gallo (and it was a small shot glass size).

Chorizo Taco= overly salted and not spicy
Carne Asada taco= dry meat and under seasoned
Al pastor taco= no comment

Charged $7 for a children's portion of rice and beans for a 5 year old. The charge was lowered after talking to the lady who stated that she just added a regular "side." $3.50 for  a side of rice at a little taqueria is excessive in the first place.

Also a bean, rice, carne asada and cheese burrito ( as plain as it gets) =$9

I was hoping Paso Robles would have a decent taqueria but I was sorely mistaken.
Try other spots.

On a lighter note The 5 year old did finish the beans</Review>
